<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:peperkoek.html>peperkoek</a> (59650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***periscoop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:periscoop.html>periscoop</a> (22456)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:periscope.html>periscope</a></i>. Postdates <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">periscopisch</i>.
